тАШSo pretty,
unsullied,
with fish for eyes,
cakrav─Бkas for beautiful breasts,
waves as eyebrows,
a lotus forming her face
and floating river weeds for streaming hair,
she is liquid sweetness.

to others her depths are menacing.
Such is the way of the profound. 90
